  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a278a0c0-396f-4551-ba6d-c56061c16195'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText162182881208547809" style="display:none"><i>An alternate cover edition can be found <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/32939730-come-away-with-me" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>.</i><br /><br />Being confronted on the beach by a sexy stranger wasn't part of Natalie Conner's plans for a peaceful morning taking photos. One thing’s for sure, he’s hot, and incredibly romantic, feeding Natalie’s wounded soul.<br /><br />Luke Williams just wants the world to give him a break, so seeing yet another camera aimed at his face has him ready to pounce on the beauty behind the lens. When he finds out she has no idea who he is, he's intrigued and more than a little tempted by her. Natalie has a body made for sex, a sassy mouth and Luke can’t get enough of her, but he’s not ready to tell her who he really his.<br /><br />Natalie is a no nonsense girl who doesn’t do well with lies and secrets. What will happen to this new relationship when she discovers what Luke’s hiding?</span>

Even the chocolate cake and the aircraft are beautiful. *facepalm*</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/library/gifs' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/404622.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>Come Away With Me</i> is one of the worst books I've read this year. Let's get down to business…<br/><br/><b>DNF at 51 %.</b> Reading this book is clearly very unhealthy for me cos I'm sure that my blood pressure went through the roof. This story is simply 'blah'. Honestly, I had to look twice when I saw all those four and five-star ratings and I thought "What is wrong </span>
  <span id="freeText947917899718371687" style="display:none"><b>Review completed November 11, 2012</b><br><br><b>46 Kindle pages refer to the term beautiful. Even the chocolate cake and the aircraft are beautiful. *facepalm*</b><br><br><a href="http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/library/gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/404622.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Come Away With Me</i> is one of the worst books I've read this year. Let's get down to business…<br><br><b>DNF at 51 %.</b> Reading this book is clearly very unhealthy for me cos I'm sure that my blood pressure went through the roof. This story is simply 'blah'. Honestly, I had to look twice when I saw all those four and five-star ratings and I thought "What is wrong with you, Baba? Did we all read the same book?" *shakes head*<br><br>I apologize to you all for using the term "shallow" pretty excessively in my review of <i>Come Away With Me.</i> While we're on it, the author applied the term 'beautiful' <b>130 times</b> in the context of <b>human beings.</b> How shallow is that?<br><br><i>His beautiful lips<br>His beautiful face <br>Oh, wait, it gets better yet: his <b>impossibly</b> beautiful face<br>He's so beautiful<br>beautiful head<br>You are so beautiful<br>beautiful body<br>She is beautiful<br>beautiful hair<br>His beautiful blue eyes<br>Good night, beautiful<br>Your sweet, beautiful ass<br>"You." Kiss. "Are." Kiss. "Beautiful."<br>You look beautiful<br>beautiful girl<br>His sister is simply beautiful<br>The granddaughter is beautiful<br>His beautiful hand</i><br><br>Of course it is very repetitive. I did not count how many times Natalie took Luke's <b>beautiful</b> face in her hand. Ugh!<br><br>Everybody is beautiful. Anything and everything is beautiful. <i>Come Away With Me</i> is <b>clearly OVERPOPULATED by beautiful and shallow people.</b> In fact, it's a shallow beauty contest and I feel like I am in the wrong movie. It's a story about shallow insta' lust &amp; "love" that did not work out for me at all. Granted, insta' lust works just fine with me when it's well done. Unfortunately the author didn't pull it off here. Hence, I never felt their chemistry and the <b>sexual tension was totally lacking</b> as well. By no stretch of the imagination was I ever able to bond with the characters either.<br><br>The cover is great but other than that I didn't like anything at all about this story. <i>Come Away With Me</i> provides shallow and one-dimensional MCs. The sex scenes are boring and poorly written and the heroine has body issues to no end from the get-go. The hero is an overly jealous fool. That said, I disliked his hot and cold attitude. And when Nat had a shooting with a client, he lost it when he thought he found them in a compromising situation. Another lame and ridiculous conflict. Finally, when Natalie was up to date about Luke being <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[a former movie star <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> she freaked out, acted childish and displayed her super drama queen attitude. Unbelievable. Absurd. <b>The writing is shallow, wooden, stilted and immature.</b><br><br><i>"God, I'm an idiot." (So true, Natalie.)<br>I'm embarrassed, I just want to run. (Yes, do that.)<br>I want him gone. (Uh-huh)<br>I want him to hold me and tell me it's not true. (Are you for real? *rolls eyes*)</i><br><br>After an unpleasant incident at his parents' house, I thought she was smart enough to realize she didn't do anything wrong. Oh, Baba, think again! They go back to his house and what does she do? Nat is insecure and she starts to tell me what <i>
  <b>he</b>
</i> might be thinking right now and <i>
  <b>that</b>
</i> is one of my pet peeves.<br><br><i>Where did he go?<br>I frown as unease starts to unfurl through my stomach. Oh my God, I really screwed up. (Duh?) He must be mad at me for the way I spoke to his sister at dinner. (*facepalm*) Where is he? (I hope he never comes back.)<br>Maybe he wants me to leave, and he's giving me space to pack my things. (I'd wish.)<br>I climb the stairs and head for his bedroom, willing myself not to cry until I get home. (Please, spare me!) I'll just pack my things and get the hell out of here. Then I can fall apart. (Just hold back till I'm gone. *rolls eyes again*)</i><br><br><a href="http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/library/gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396630ra/764794.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>"No one has ever jumped to my defense like that. You were so calm and sure of yourself, and so pissed off. Your green eyes were on fire, and you looked so beautiful. (blah...*rolls eyes once more*) I wanted to f@ck you right there at the table." (*gasp*)<br>"Luke Williams!" I pull back and stare at him, shocked.<br>"It's true. You turned me on, big time." (Really?)<br>"I don't think that would have been appropriate with your parents sitting at that same table." (Truer words have never been spoken.)<br>"I don't think I would have cared if the Pope and Elvis were sitting at that table." (I'm sure the Pope would have had a heart attack and Elvis is turning over in his grave right now.</i><br><br>Frankly, I completely understand that some people get off on voyeurism. But. What Luke said was simply disgusting. Doing the deed in front of his parents? No, thanks.<br><br><b>Overall verdict</b><br><i>Come Away With Me</i> is a huge disappointment and one of the worst books I've read this year. Read at your own risk.<br><br><br><b>A shout out to my GR friend Tammy<br> 51 Kindle pages</b> refer to your beloved term 'baby'. Got it, baby? *angelic smile* <br><br><br><b>Steam: 3 / Chemistry: 0 / Sensuality: 0 / Eroticism: 0</b><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5321255646186307425">I don’t even have to think twice…what was one of the worst books I read this year…..Come Away with Me, the 1st book in Kristen Proby’s With me in Seattle Series.<br/><br/>After seeing all those 4 and 5 star ratings….I asked myself….is this the same book I read????? I gave up halfway….and that’s saying something about me….because I do not like DNF reading a book!!! But seriously, I could not turn another page and read about how beautiful Natalie Conner is and how beautiful….<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448558076ra/17158800.gif' alt=' photo giphy_zpscda1pzsg.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>.<br/>Oops, sorry, the hero in this s</span>
  <span id="freeText5321255646186307425" style="display:none">I don’t even have to think twice…what was one of the worst books I read this year…..Come Away with Me, the 1st book in Kristen Proby’s With me in Seattle Series.<br><br>After seeing all those 4 and 5 star ratings….I asked myself….is this the same book I read????? I gave up halfway….and that’s saying something about me….because I do not like DNF reading a book!!! But seriously, I could not turn another page and read about how beautiful Natalie Conner is and how beautiful….<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448558076ra/17158800.gif" alt=" photo giphy_zpscda1pzsg.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">.<br>Oops, sorry, the hero in this story is not Edward Cullen…I just got a bit confused with the hero, whose name is Luke Williams, who happens to be an ex super movie star who acted in 3 blockbuster movies about vampires…..apologies for the mistake!<br><br>Okay, let me start again!<br><br>Natalie is taking fotos on the beach early one morning when she’s suddenly confronted by the most BEAUTIFUL man who wants to rip her camera from her and demands why she’s taking fotos of him. Of course, she’s taken no photos of the guy…even though he’s beyond beautiful.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448558076ra/17158801.gif" alt=" photo hessobeautiful_zpsuqwbakhr.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So, everything is sorted out eventually and Luke Williams, hiding his famous identity from Natalie, is suddenly struck with lust for the sexy Natalie…..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448558076ra/17158802.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_n7sgx0qD6K1rxoktf_zpsao9quyho.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Natalie is just as struck with lust for Luke…..he’s beautiful, he’s gorgeous, he’s beautiful<blockquote><b><i>“Clearly, Mr Beautiful Blue Eyes and Sexy Greek God Face is a loony tune.” </i></b></blockquote>Hell, Luke Williams is doing something to me…..never mind to poor old Natalie, with all her body issues!!!!! She can’t believe this Greek god thinks she’s beautiful. A guy like him……<blockquote><b><i>““I’ve fallen in love with a beautiful, sexy, sweet, jealous control freak.<br>Shit.” </i></b></blockquote>My head is spinning….Luke Williams is causing me some problems…..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448558076ra/17158803.gif" alt=" photo you are so beautiful gif_zps5wvp1gyn.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Right, insta-love occurs. These two people are beyond besotted with their beautiful partners…..<br><br>Sorry, am I repeating myself???? Just want to make it very clear that these are extraordinary BEAUTIFUL people, who are so in love…..a real LOVE STORY here!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448558076ra/17158804.gif" alt=" photo you-are-so-beautiful_861_zpsh7izsuvd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>By now it should be clear how the word BEAUTIFUL applies to EVERYONE and I mean EVERYONE in this story….the hero/heroine are beautiful, the heroine’s bff is beautiful, the hero’s mother, father, sister are beautiful….in fact, these people are totally superficial and so not deep…but never mind…because……<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448558076ra/17158805.gif" alt=" photo ariana-grande-everyone-is-beautiful-avan-jogia-gif_zpsqsprakwv.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>All the drama, all the jealousy…………hell, never mind having my fingers in my mouth half way through this story…it was more of something like this….<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448558076ra/17158806.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m6yrn9ZVCV1qh2o7zo1_500_zps86mt68gp.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This is the 1st book I read by this author…….am I going to read any other by her??? Not sure!!! But what I am sure is that I don’t think I will continue with this series.<br><br>Of course, there are so many other readers who loved this book……and I totally understand that it works for some…for me….it did not!!!!</span>

<div id="review_624631295" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/624631295" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/624631295?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=pregnant-heroines">pregnant-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer624631295" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8085165296317587070"><strong>A Nice, Predictable Romance</strong><br/><br/>As far as sweet, heartwarming romances go, this was a pretty good choice. It was predictable, but enjoyable. I listened to the Audible version and found the narration to be well done as well.<br/><br/>Natalie meets Luke when she is taking pictures early one morning. She is a photographer and he mistakenly thinks that she is photographing him. He tries to get her camera from her, only to find out that he had misjudged the situation.<br/><br/>There is plenty of attraction between the two an</span>
  <span id="freeText8085165296317587070" style="display:none"><strong>A Nice, Predictable Romance</strong><br /><br />As far as sweet, heartwarming romances go, this was a pretty good choice. It was predictable, but enjoyable. I listened to the Audible version and found the narration to be well done as well.<br /><br />Natalie meets Luke when she is taking pictures early one morning. She is a photographer and he mistakenly thinks that she is photographing him. He tries to get her camera from her, only to find out that he had misjudged the situation.<br /><br />There is plenty of attraction between the two and a whirlwind romance ensues. Yet, before they can even establish their relationship, they are having problems. After only a day or two together, they're having their first big fight. From that point forward there is drama, drama, drama!<br /><br />Now, I love stories with a large helping of conflict and plenty of angst. However, you really can get too much of a good thing. The deeper into this story I got, the more I wondered if there was any cliche that hadn't been covered. It felt like the author just started throwing in every over-used plot "twist" that could be thought of, indiscriminately. One or two is manageable, but this was out of hand. <br /><br />Despite all of that, I did mostly enjoy this story. It was good, even if I spent a fair amount of time rolling my eyes. In fact, the first half was easily a 4-star read for me. Somewhere along the way, it fumbled.<br /><br />I won't be rereading this one, but it was alright for a one-time listen. Could've been better, but it could've been a lot worse also. This one landed firmly in the "middle of the road" territory for me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8085165296317587070" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_448084448" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/448084448" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/448084448?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer448084448" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2179857024339686416"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794968i/599118.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>HOLY FREAKING SWOON!! <br/><br/>Looking for a steamy, no angst, pure swoon-fest?? Look no further!<br/><br/>I still can’t believe this was a debut novel! The flow, the writing style, the feel of the story, the characters, everything just instantly hooked me from the first scene. Seriously, I read most of this book with this happy little smile on my face and my heart a-fluttering.<br/><br/>On a beautiful quiet morning, Natalie is out on the beach taking photos of the scenery when she is suddenly confronted by a gorgeous man e</span>
  <span id="freeText2179857024339686416" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794968i/599118.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>HOLY FREAKING SWOON!! <br><br>Looking for a steamy, no angst, pure swoon-fest?? Look no further!<br><br>I still can’t believe this was a debut novel! The flow, the writing style, the feel of the story, the characters, everything just instantly hooked me from the first scene. Seriously, I read most of this book with this happy little smile on my face and my heart a-fluttering.<br><br>On a beautiful quiet morning, Natalie is out on the beach taking photos of the scenery when she is suddenly confronted by a gorgeous man enraged that she was taking his picture and demanding that she turn over her camera. Clearly surprised that she actually wasn’t, and even more shocked (and thrilled) that she doesn’t know who he is, and he apologizes profusely and asks her out to breakfast hoping to smooth over their rough start.<br><br>And so begins their relationship. Luke loves that Natalie doesn’t recognize him and that her feelings for him are based purely on what he’s shown her of himself, and Natalie can’t get enough of this amazing, charming man who stepped into her life. But Natalie is a up front, honest girl and when she eventually finds out what he’s hiding, the sparks fly.<br><br><b> <i> “Are you having doubts?”<br>“Hell, no, I just want to make sure this is what you want, baby. If you say no, that’s fine, but please, God, don’t say no.” </i> </b><br><br>Luke. Oh my god Luke freaking Williams! I have a new book boyfriend (shhh, don’t tell the others)! He was butterflies-in-my-belly, set-my-heart-a-flutter, clutch-my-chest-and-fan-myself swoony! He cooked, opened doors, gave foot rubs, bought flowers (by the truckload), planed surprises, spoiled his girl… and best of all, was completely devoted to and in love with Natalie. Over all, pretty much just pure fantasy man material.<br><br><i> “Is there anyone else?”<br>“Why is that any of your business?”<br>“Because you’re the first woman I’ve brought into my home and all I can think about is getting your beautiful body naked and fucking you senseless. I need to know if there is any competition. I don’t share, Natalie.”…<br>“Saying that you don’t want to share implies that I’m already yours, Luke.”<br>“Aren’t you?” he whispers.” </i><br><br>Their relationship was very romantic, very quick to develop (remember, this book is pure swoon-fest), and very functional. They each had their insecurities but I really liked how they compromised in each situation. Neither of them would just roll over and give in but would each listen to the other’s perspective and make a decision that respected their feelings.<br><br>This book has no external drama or bad guy. No cheating, major stupidity, long separations or anything will make you threaten bodily harm to your eReader. Its solely focused on the romance between Luke and Natalie!<br><br>And oh my Lord are there ever boat-loads of steamy sex scenes! Seriously, these guys can’t stop doing it! =) Everywhere! The wall, the bed, the bathroom, the shower, the limo, the airplane, the desk, the car, the beach… I’m sure I’m missing a few but this book basically goes from swoon to sex to swoon to sex to more swoon and more sex… mostly vanilla but all hottt!<br><br>The book is told in first person perspective from Natalie’s POV for the whole story up until the very sweet epilogue which is from Luke. The writing style was vaguely reminiscent of EL James’ in places. I kind of wavered on whether or not that was a good thing but overall, I guess the fact that I honestly smiled my way through most of the book meant that I really liked it. I love the style and it worked well for this story.<br><br><i> “I’ve fallen in love with a beautiful, sexy, sweet, jealous control freak.<br>Shit.” </i><br><br>So given all the boat-loads of swoon and steam, what made it 4 stars instead of 5? There were a few small things, nothing huge, though but there were a few moments that made me give the page the “squinty skeptical eye” and go hrmmmm (but nothing lingering, just kind of a moment that I got over quickly). I also found there was a bit too much focus on body image talk – at first it was fine, but it was mentioned several times over the course of the book and eventually got to be a little much for me. And while the heroine was definitely not what I’d call annoying, she did have a few (luckily, very short) moments that made me roll my eyes. And lastly, and this might sound weird, but some parts of the story just felt a little ‘too’ perfect at times. Too many endearments, too many 'perfect' scenes. But still, I mean, for a pure swoon-fest, that’s kind of what you want, right? :D<br><br>This book left me completely satisfied with Luke and Natalie's story. There is a HEA (no cliffhanger!) and I'm very much looking forward to more from this author. And she just told me we have a LOT to look forward to: Book #2 "Fight With Me" which will follow Jules' (the best friend's) and Nate's story and is scheduled for release on Jan 4, 2013. Then Will's story, "Play With Me" comes out in March!!! oh, and we get an Isaac/Stacy novella this December too! Seriously, Kristen Proby sure knows how to keep her readers happy :D<br><br>If you love steamy romance without excess drama, then definitely add this book to your TBRs! <br><br><i> Thank you to the author Kristen Proby for providing me with an ARC of this novel in exchange for an honest review. </i> <br><br>CASTING (above and below)<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396445i/764190._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2179857024339686416" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

When I started this, I thought the dialog was a little corny and that it was not going to be a hit with me. In the end, I truly ended up enjoying this one so much!!!<br/><br/><br/><br/>Natalie is a photographer and Luke was once a Major Hollywood actor.   <span id="freeText368630128837318758" style="display:none"><b>*****FOUR STARS*****</b><br>{BR with Mel}<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/11deb066c61c29de8b88e219d9536d1e_zpsbetrmyuu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432444285i/14961693._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 11deb066c61c29de8b88e219d9536d1e_zpsbetrmyuu.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I have had this book on my TBR since 2012 and decided to read it since I'll be meeting Ms Proby at a book signing in NYC next weekend! When I started this, I thought the dialog was a little corny and that it was not going to be a hit with me. In the end, I truly ended up enjoying this one so much!!!<br><br><br><br>Natalie is a photographer and Luke was once a Major Hollywood actor. He hasn't acted in several years and loves his life of seclusion in Seattle. When the two meet, they don't hit it off instantly, as Luke mistakes Natalie for a Paparazzi and tries to confiscate her camera. In her line of work she takes sexy boudoir pictures of couples and she also just takes pictures of the local scenery. She's not into movies so she has no clue that Luke was once a box office draw. This, of course, intrigues and captivates him.<br><br><br><br>This story is very predictable. At times I compared it to <b>"Love Unscripted"</b>, although I wouldn't put them in the same caliber. I knew exactly what was going to happen when it did happen. But, funny enough, I really freaking enjoyed this story more than I ever thought possible. I loved Luke and his sexy, possessive and alpha ways. There was plenty of steamy sex. And I really liked some of the secondary characters. I am looking forward to reading Jules' book some time soon.<br><br><br><br>If you are in need for something light with plenty of steamy sex and some lovable characters, I would definitely recommend this to you!! :)</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=mile-high-club">mile-high-club</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer448142428" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6337311677048320020"><b>Holy Hotness Batman!</b><br/><br/>This is a stunningly sexy, super steamy contemporary romance and I adore the gorgeous, enticing cover.<br/><br/>Natalie, a professional photographer, and Luke have very inauspicious beginnings on the beach early one morning when she is out taking photographs. He sees red and accuses her of taking pictures of him when she is, in fact, taking landscape shots. Luke has reasons to want to protect his privacy but Nat just thinks he’s a mugger trying to steal her camera. It’s a case of beaut</span>
  <span id="freeText6337311677048320020" style="display:none"><b>Holy Hotness Batman!</b><br><br>This is a stunningly sexy, super steamy contemporary romance and I adore the gorgeous, enticing cover.<br><br>Natalie, a professional photographer, and Luke have very inauspicious beginnings on the beach early one morning when she is out taking photographs. He sees red and accuses her of taking pictures of him when she is, in fact, taking landscape shots. Luke has reasons to want to protect his privacy but Nat just thinks he’s a mugger trying to steal her camera. It’s a case of beautiful mugger meets beautiful artist.<br><br>After apologising profusely for his actions when he realises his mistake, Luke relishes Nat's ignorance of who he is and, as their relationship develops, he loves that she is coming to care for him, the real Luke as a person without pre-conceived ideas. Of course, he’s lying to her by omission and you can expect sparks to fly when she eventually finds out.<br><br>Luke is a hero to die for – he’s attentive, romantic, pretty nifty between the sheets and really quite devoted to Nat. He’s a beautiful, sexy, sweet, jealous control freak. Nat has known her share of heartbreak and is slow to trust but she soon opens up to Luke and shares her darkest secrets with him and she is a worthy heroine – fiery, loyal and tenacious. She’s not going to take any crap from anyone, however rich they are and certainly puts Luke through his paces.<br><br>Their story is incredibly steamy and this is an erotic romance that has more sex scenes than you can shake a stick at! Nat has a collection of script tattoos all over her body in places that are hidden by her clothes and the scene where Luke slowly discovers them all is quite the sensual voyage of discovery! Their story is stunning – two wounded souls finding salvation together, healing one another. Despite being very sexy, it’s also a beautiful romance and the epilogue is absolutely to die for as it’s told from Luke’s POV, after the whole novel is told from Nat’s.<br><br>This is highly recommended for all you erotic romanceaholics out there. You know who you are!<br><br>Nat &amp; Luke<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396453i/764209._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There’s a great host of richly, crafted secondary characters who add great depth and detail to the story and I’m seriously hoping that Nat’s best friend, Jules will star in a sequel with Nate.<br><br><i>With thanks to the lovely Kristen Proby for providing me with an ARC of this novel<br><br>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a></i><br><br>Come Away With Me goes on sale Friday November 9th 2012</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/428938882?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gitte TotallyBookedBlog" href="/user/show/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog">Gitte TotallyBookedBlog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7379751-gitte-totallybookedblog?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer428938882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16750239556905017513">This book was a 2.5 star read for me.<br/><br/>I have to say I was really looking forward to reading this book with my fellow readers on our blog. The hype surrounding it had been immense and from what I had heard everyone was loving it. I was sent an arc for an honest review by the Author a while back but I decided to wait and read it with everyone else as is normally the case with BOFF reads; which I love.<br/><br/>Unfortunately I didn't love it, and I hate when that happens because I know how much an Author puts</span>
  <span id="freeText16750239556905017513" style="display:none">This book was a 2.5 star read for me.<br /><br />I have to say I was really looking forward to reading this book with my fellow readers on our blog. The hype surrounding it had been immense and from what I had heard everyone was loving it. I was sent an arc for an honest review by the Author a while back but I decided to wait and read it with everyone else as is normally the case with BOFF reads; which I love.<br /><br />Unfortunately I didn't love it, and I hate when that happens because I know how much an Author puts into their story. However, there are so many amazing books out there and I have my integrity and always endeavour to leave an honest review no matter how much it pains me to do so like in this case.<br /><br />So yeah, this one didn't work for me. I was enjoying the start and thought this is going to be good, then I lost it and I have to admit to skim reading through the middle until the last bit where it picked up again. So overall, I guess I could stretch to saying it was just okay.<br /><br />To me, and this is my opinion, it was gratuitous sex with no real story to balance it out. Like a mediocre badly dubbed porn flick where the words baby and beautiful lost all meaning. Do I love my sexy steamy books, absolutely 100% yes, however I need a story too, I need the emotions, the angst, the connection with the characters and I just didn't get that. I wanted to love this story so much, as everyone else seems to but on no reflection on the Author, it just wasn't for me.<br /><br />I really liked how Luke and Natalie met, and I really did think Natalie was a lovely character whereas Luke blew hot and cold for me but I just couldn't connect to either characters. <br /><br />I will say that I did enjoy the ending and I thought the Author pulled it back in, on way to redeeming it somewhat for me, but it was just that little bit to late. <br /><br />I'm going to call this a marmite book; you either love it or you don't.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16750239556905017513" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_452906165" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/452906165" />
    <a title="twstrfries" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2960653-twstrfries"><img alt="twstrfries" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1567873767p2/2960653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/452906165?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="twstrfries" class="user" itemprop="url" name="twstrfries" href="/user/show/2960653-twstrfries">twstrfries</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2960653-twstrfries?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2960653-twstrfries?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2960653-twstrfries?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2960653-twstrfries?shelf=celebrity-rich-and-famous">celebrity-rich-and-famous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2960653-twstrfries?shelf=2012">2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer452906165" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16173787888614790646">I'm starting to hate random downloads. It’s a game of hit or miss and I'm getting a lot of misses lately. I like trying out Indie authors. You can never tell when you'll find a gem in a sea of e-books today, that's why I give them a try. But now I think I need a break.<br/><br/><i>Come Away with Me</i> has a nice cover and blurb. I'm still crazy-craving-for-celebrity-characters so I picked this up. Oh my, what a freaking waste of time. I know how much authors invest in their work but this really didn't work for </span>
  <span id="freeText16173787888614790646" style="display:none">I'm starting to hate random downloads. It’s a game of hit or miss and I'm getting a lot of misses lately. I like trying out Indie authors. You can never tell when you'll find a gem in a sea of e-books today, that's why I give them a try. But now I think I need a break.<br /><br /><i>Come Away with Me</i> has a nice cover and blurb. I'm still crazy-craving-for-celebrity-characters so I picked this up. Oh my, what a freaking waste of time. I know how much authors invest in their work but this really didn't work for me. <br /><br />- The plot is common, no serious conflict. <br />- There are events that were thrown in from out of nowhere and at times all at once without even making the characters breathe. <br />- The author has a lot of ideas and she crammed it in the first book of a series. <br />- The world building was not realistic. The author failed to catch the reality of Hollywood. <br />- The characters didn't stand out. They're flat. <br />- The sex isn't even good. Bleh.<br /><br />I don't consider the bad plot and storytelling enough reasons for me to give this a 1-star rating. What ticks me most was the writing. There are a lot of grammar slips I can't make myself not to notice. There are also details that aren't necessary. It gives the impression that the writing is aimed to impress not to express.<br /><br />Another issue I can't let go is the pregnancy. This particular sentence made my head spin:<br /><br /><i>"I'm on the pill to prevent pregnancy"</i><br /><br />Duh?! It’s a contraceptive for chrissake. What do you think it is for? World peace? That's the main reason of using the Pill unless stated otherwise. The explanation of it not working is unbelievable after the heroine strongly claimed that she never missed a pill and that she is taking it correctly. The doctor insisted that it's 99.9% effective when it’s taken correctly <i>(he's not listening, is he?)</i> and sadly she is part of the 1%. Can I get a better explanation? Like maybe the patient took antibiotics that wane its effectiveness?<br /><br />I really should take a break from reading Indie adult contemporary romance. Huh.<br /><br /><br />****<br /><i>Review also posted @ <b><a href="http://shanatalks.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Off the Wall</a></b>.</i></span>

<div id="review_450036096" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/450036096" />
    <a title="Holly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2127955-holly"><img alt="Holly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520179670p2/2127955.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/450036096?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Holly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Holly" href="/user/show/2127955-holly">Holly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=obsessively-readable">obsessively-readable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=sweet-hero">sweet-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=favorite-heroes">favorite-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=6-star-books">6-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=best-books-read-in-2013">best-books-read-in-2013</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer450036096" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8681725310589768607"><b>6 gushtastic stars</b><br/><br/>The perfect blend of sweet, angst-free romance and super hot sex. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396748ra/765056.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have had this book for quite a while, and to be honest...after reading some of the less than stellar reviews I kept pushing it down my TBR list.<br/>If I have learned anything from this experience it's that I really need to ignore other people's reviews and go with my own gut instinct, because in the end...I absolutely <b>adored</b> this book.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/580530.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Confession time: When i started reading this book, it took me a while to get past</span>
  <span id="freeText8681725310589768607" style="display:none"><b>6 gushtastic stars</b><br><br>The perfect blend of sweet, angst-free romance and super hot sex. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396748ra/765056.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have had this book for quite a while, and to be honest...after reading some of the less than stellar reviews I kept pushing it down my TBR list.<br>If I have learned anything from this experience it's that I really need to ignore other people's reviews and go with my own gut instinct, because in the end...I absolutely <b>adored</b> this book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/580530.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Confession time: When i started reading this book, it took me a while to get past a couple of issues that i had. First of all, in the beginning it really felt like fanfiction to me. Not to say that the writing wasn't enjoyable to read...it was just that something felt a little off...which brings me to the other issue that i had. From the very first scene in which Natalie stumbles upon him, I had the impression that the author had based Luke's character on Rob Pattinson. And then...I read this.<br><br><i>
  <b>Luke had stared in three vampire movies that not only did well, but became such a huge sensation that you couldn't go anywhere without seeing the stars or merchandise of all kinds. </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396748ra/765057.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But you know what? After that revelation, something amazing happened. I put the whole idea of fanfic and Edward Cullen out of my head...and lost myself in the story. Because what Kristen Proby did was bring to life an incredibly sweet, and blessedly angst-free love story that completely blew me away. And offered up more swoon-worthy moments than almost any other book I have ever read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396748i/765058.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396748i/765059._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396748i/765060._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Luke is...hands down...<b>the most romantic male character I have ever stumbled upon in fiction.</b> Some of the things he does for Natalie almost made me cry because they were so overwhelmingly sweet. But not roll-your-eyes-to-the-back-of-your-head kind of sweet. No, Luke's sweetness was...just right in the scope of this incredibly romantic story, if that makes any sense?! <br><br>Something else that I absolutely loved about this book is that Natalie is not a stick-figure. She has curves, and Luke never stops letting Natalie know how much he appreciates those curves. It was refreshing to me to read about a man who appreciates a <i>real</i> woman's body. And while I will always love my bad boys, it was so nice to read about a guy who was head over heels in love with his girl and wanted the whole world to know it.<br><br>And did I mention the fact that i <b>loved</b> the lack of angst?! God, talk about a breath of fresh air! I for one have read way too many books where the H/h flip flop on their feelings and torture themselves (and the reader) with their (mostly self imposed) struggles to be together. Natalie and Luke embrace their feelings for each other and even though I realize the speed at which their relationship progresses may annoy some people, for me it felt natural. <br><br><b>
  <i>"You are every fantasy I have ever had come true, Natalie...<br>I'm almost afraid to touch you," he whispers.<br>"Why?" I cock my head to the side, confused.<br>"I'm afraid you're not real." </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396748ra/765061.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In case you're beginning to think that there was no heat in this book...let me set your mind at ease. The sex scenes are hot! And yes, there are a lot of them. Luke and Natalie's chemistry is insane right from the beginning. If I was going to be nit-picky, I would admit that I got a little tired of reading the word 'impressive' when Natalie was thinking about a certain part of Luke's body, and the sheer number of times that Luke commented on how wet Natalie was. But again...that's being nit-picky. :P<br><br><i>Come Away With Me</i> was a beautiful, swoon fest of a book. I was truly sad to see Luke &amp; Natalie's story come to an end, because I loved being lost inside their world. &lt;3<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380735205i/3116707.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>He leans down and gently presses his cheek to mine. "Thank you," he whispers.<br>"For what?" I whisper back.<br>"For being mine."</b>
</i><br><br>Read more of my reviews at my blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://ravingbookaddict.blogspot.com/">http://ravingbookaddict.blogspot.com/</a></span>

<div id="review_529974338" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/529974338" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/529974338?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=hyped">hyped</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=recommendations">recommendations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=z-no-bueno">z-no-bueno</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=everyone-loved-but-duchess">everyone-loved-but-duchess</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer529974338" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6111070757071862313">2.5 Stars<br/>I knew going in to this that it wouldn't be a favorite of mine, but I'm a stickler for reading order. And it wasn't necessarily HORRIBLE. In fact, I can see the appeal for some readers. But I've been much more stingy with stars as of late, and this book just didn't cut it. So 2.5 Stars...<br/><br/><b>
  <u>My Synopsis:</u>
</b><br/>Natalie is a photographer living in...you guessed it, Seattle. One fine morning while walking along the beach, snapping photos of the beauty that surrounds her, she is suddenly assaulted</span>
  <span id="freeText6111070757071862313" style="display:none">2.5 Stars<br />I knew going in to this that it wouldn't be a favorite of mine, but I'm a stickler for reading order. And it wasn't necessarily HORRIBLE. In fact, I can see the appeal for some readers. But I've been much more stingy with stars as of late, and this book just didn't cut it. So 2.5 Stars...<br /><br /><b>
  <u>My Synopsis:</u>
</b><br />Natalie is a photographer living in...you guessed it, Seattle. One fine morning while walking along the beach, snapping photos of the beauty that surrounds her, she is suddenly assaulted by some strange, huge, HOT man who is apparently enraged with her. He is adamant that she not take his picture. Once Natalie finally convinces the loony that she was indeed only out for nature pics and other non personal photos, he does your basic one eighty and asks her out. Of course, our smart girl wants nothing to do with the crazy man, and politely refuses.<br /><br />When Natalie runs into Luke again a few days later, he is adamant that she get coffee with him, and Natalie finally agrees. Little does she know that the yummy male hotness that she starts to see on a regular basis is none other than Luke Williams, famous actor now gone reclusive due to a kind of phobia concerning fans and paparazzi. For the longest time, she doesn't figure it out. And when she finally does, the angst begins...and doesn't end...<br /><br /><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br />My biggest problem was how much sex there was. Now, don't get me wrong...I like sex in books. In fact, I LOVE sex in books...when it's done right. In Come Away With me, there was seriously a sex scene in nearly every other scene in the book. <br /><br />Go to lunch....have sex<br />Go to dinner....have sex<br />Meet your parents....have sex<br />Meet your roommate....have sex<br />Have a fight....have sex<br />Take a shower....have sex<br />Walk downstairs....have sex <br />Smile funny....have sex<br />Breath....have sex<br /><br />It was seriously redundant. Not to mention that the sex was soooo boring and mediocre. These two have sex like they've already been married for ten years and the lust is gone. Most of the sex scenes themselves lasted for only one page or so and consisted of a brief kiss, rubbing of chest or breasts, possibly a little oral action, and a quick thrust or two before a guaranteed orgasm... I prefer <i>quality sex</i> to lots of sex. Give me one ten page love scene with tons of description, slow, aching movements, and a drawn out climax to ten short and sweet sex scenes that feel like a handful of slam, bam, thank you ma'ams.<br /><br />There just wasn't much room left for a fully fleshed out plot. What there WAS of the plot was a good one. I liked both Luke and Natalie a lot. Neither was stupid, neither was thoughtless. They fit together well. I like the families...I LOVE the fact that each of them have a supportive, loving group of people that will continue to be a part of this series. <br /><br />There were a few other things that bugged me. I get frustrated at medical stuff being thrown in but not researched properly. (Hyperemesis gravidarum is usually a VERY serious situation for pregnant women, and here it was glossed over as if it could be taken care of with an anti-nausea pill. Very much not so in real life.)<br /><br />I'm going to stop here, because I don't want to come across as nit picky. Suffice it to say, if I didn't have a few of my friends assuring me that this series gets better, I'd likely have stopped right here. I really had to push on through to finish this one. However, I really do see potential in this author. I understand that this was a debut novel for her...please correct me if I'm wrong...and she has since moved on to get better and better ratings/reviews. So I'm still very excited to read the next installment!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6111070757071862313" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText8997872011140080279" style="display:none">This was a 2.5 possibly 3 for me. <br /><br />I had a few issues with the relationship between the 2 main characters.<br /><br />Natalie Conner is a photographer who is confronted one morning, while taking pictures, by Luke Williams, who thinks she is taking his picture.<br /><br />It was a nice set up for a nice light read<br /><br />However <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ There were times I wanted Natalie's best friend to tell her to run, run far away from this man!<br /><br />On the first day they meet Luke goes from being playful and charming to serious and looking like he has been kicked in the stomach, for no apparent reason. Other than the fact he is apparently at this point hiding some great secret. <br /><br />Again, the first time they are having drinks together, after having only met that day, she offers to pay for her own drink and<i> "he glares at me, an I'm stunned that he looks genuinely mad"</i><br /><br />He is very full on straight away.<i> "all I can think about is getting your beautiful body naked and fucking you senseless. I need to know if there is any competition. I don't share Natalie"</i><br /><br />Again on their very first day together, the day they met, he gets angry when she gets a txt from a friend/ex FWB. He aks who he is, and when she says he is just a friend he is <i>"Look at me" His voice is sharp</i><br /><br /><br />He is snarling at her on their second day of knowing her when she admits she does not date men, or has not in the past, only slept with them. Ok, it might not sound good, but they have known each other just over 24 hours at this point!<br /><br />When it comes out who he is, and Natalie gets upset and runs to her bedroom, he hits the wall and shouts at her <i>"OPEN THE MOTHERFUCKING DOOR"</i> I think they have reached 48 hours of knowing each other at this point.<br /><br />He then sends literally dozens upon dozens on roses to say sorry and she is all <i>"Oh my. Have the inevitable misunderstanding that leads one or the other to think the other is cheating. Check<br />4. Have the accidental pregnancy. Check<br />5. Check<br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />So all in all, a 2.5 at most 3 star for me.   <span id="freeText11172581810654310236" style="display:none">3.5 Stars.. Did I like this book ? Yes.. did I love it? Unfortunitly, no.. The first quarter of the book was really good.. I really liked how Luke and Natalie met on the beach--that was really cute. The chemistry was for sure there in the beginning, and throughout the book but come mid ways through the book it just all seemed repetitious.. Meet at Nats house, have sex , meet at Lukes house, have sex, back and forth. Don't get me wrong, the sex scenes were really steamy and sweet, but sometimes the talking was just wierd.. him constantly saying "my love" or " come, my love".. not come as in "come here" but come as in the big O. Just seemed wierd.. " come my love". Luke whined a lot and was very jealous and it was not a sexy alpha jealous.. it was like a whiney baby jealous. All in all, it was a good fluff read, something to kind of clean my pallet of the angsty YA's i've been reading lately. There was not too much to think abour or worry about or wonder about.. I would probably classify this one as a good beach read. I was going back and forth with it.. sometimes was really in to it, then I would struggle with getting through a few chapters. Alot of people have really liked it though.. </span>

I've got 3 words for this story or more like 3 words to describe how I feel about this story !<br><br><b> SWEET , SIMPLE &amp; SEXY !!!! </b> <br><br>I have to say that Kristen Proby has definitely hit the nail on the head with this one in the ' SWEETNESS OVERLOAD ' department ! The book is a fun filled , no tension filled heart breaking angsty type of a read at all . Instead , it just focuses on this super cute couple who enjoy being in love , and try to get pass various insecurities and past issues . <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=phil-dunphy-thumbsup.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394501ra/759487.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The blurb pretty much says everything that needs to be said , but you seriously have to read this book and see what its all about ! You are sure to fall in love with it ! <br><br>Natalie and Luke are just AWESOME !! They are in love and very new to this feeling . What I mean is that although they've been in relationships before , this - what they have/feel for each other - is new to them and I loved the way their relationship progressed in this story . <br><br>The romance here is a pretty good mix of sweet and steamy . Luke is this scorchingly hot and sinfully tempting smooth operator who loves pearls and roses ! I was all like , ' Ohmygod !! Iwantaboyfriendjustlikehim !!! ' * wishful thinking * and Natalie , I would love to be BFF's with her for sure !! <br><br>One moment the romance is like :<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m8kbz4arh21raw1kzo1_500.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394501ra/759488.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>and the next its all :<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=Damn.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394501ra/759489.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Damn I love this book . After I finished reading it , I was a sloppy mess of happy tears and hope ! Yeah , this book makes you want to believe that love exists , that one day you'll find your prince charming and that one day love will surely come around ! * Wipes tears * <br><br>Kristen Proby makes an impressive debut , and I'm sure as fuck that I'll be reading more of her works !!! Come Away With Me is a sweetly told , sexily sketched story of finding love and believing in it !<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7813298541948158278" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_461888255" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/461888255" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/461888255?book_show_action=true">Nov 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer461888255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6320406173863202010">Come Away with me is a sexy, steamy, and swoony contemporary romance.<br/><br/>Natalie is a photographer who is out early taking photos at the beach when she is confronted by a hot guy yelling at her for her camera. At first she thinks he is trying to mug her, but when he calms down after looking at her photos and explains that he values his privacy and thought she was taking photos of him, it gets cleared up.<br/>Luke feels terrible for acting the way he did and being thrilled that Natalie doesn't know who he</span>
  <span id="freeText6320406173863202010" style="display:none">Come Away with me is a sexy, steamy, and swoony contemporary romance.<br /><br />Natalie is a photographer who is out early taking photos at the beach when she is confronted by a hot guy yelling at her for her camera. At first she thinks he is trying to mug her, but when he calms down after looking at her photos and explains that he values his privacy and thought she was taking photos of him, it gets cleared up.<br />Luke feels terrible for acting the way he did and being thrilled that Natalie doesn't know who he is, he asks her out for breakfast. She says no, but later in the day they run into each other again and end up going out for drinks. They are both extremely attracted to one another and end up spending a lot of time together. As their relationship develops, Natalie really opens up to Luke in a way she never has before, at the same time, he isn't being honest with her about who he really is...<br /><br />Luke Williams... Wow. What a charming and swoony guy! He was almost too perfect. He was romantic, spoils her, cooks for her, gets her Starbucks delivered (that would win my heart) and the roses, foot rubs, and of course his many other talents... It's no wonder Natalie falls for him so easily!<br /><i>"I've fallen in love with a beautiful,sexy, sweet, jealous control freak. Shit."</i><br />Natalie is a likable and relatable character. She has had tragedy in her life and doesn't get too close to a lot of people. Love her her hidden tattoos. She is loyal and feisty (when she went off on Luke's sister :-) Luke and Natalie both had great family and friends that contributed a lot to the story.<br /><br />This story was sweet, romantic, and steamy... Holy wow was it steamy! And Luke had to be one of the most swoony guys ever! The cover is stunning, and the lack of major angst/drama was a nice change. Great ending, especially the epilogue in Luke's pov &lt;3 excited to start Jules and Nate's story: Fight with me...<br />Read &amp; enjoy!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6320406173863202010" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of feel-good erotic romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer728952242" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2687464079409130679">Sometimes I thought the hero, former movie idol Luke (who had professional similarities to Robert Pattinson but no way did he look like him) was almost too good to be true (sweet, kind, generous, protective, incredibly sexy) and at other times I thought this guy might be hard to live with, because he was also a little <i>too</i> protective, needy, insecure, and with a jealous streak. But I've seen him in the later books (one advantage of reading the books way out of order) and he seems to be falling in</span>
  <span id="freeText2687464079409130679" style="display:none">Sometimes I thought the hero, former movie idol Luke (who had professional similarities to Robert Pattinson but no way did he look like him) was almost too good to be true (sweet, kind, generous, protective, incredibly sexy) and at other times I thought this guy might be hard to live with, because he was also a little <i>too</i> protective, needy, insecure, and with a jealous streak. But I've seen him in the later books (one advantage of reading the books way out of order) and he seems to be falling in the too-good-to-be-true category. So yeah, he's totally swoon-worthy to me.<br><br><i>Luke...you just kept bringing Paul Walker to mind...</i><br><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/aunteecr051/paulwalker2_zps3bc3626c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388884826i/7949863.jpg" alt=" photo paulwalker2_zps3bc3626c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I liked the book, and the whole series so far, even though there's not a whole lot of conflict going on. Just a whole lot of hot sex, some minor misunderstandings, and for the most part, the H/h have no problems expressing their love for one another. Basically just some feel good romances.<br><br>If I had one complaint about the whole series so far (and this is minor though irksome) I wish the author would employ a better editor, one who knows something about grammar. I thought maybe this was just going to be a problem in the first book, but I see it's carried on the whole series.<br><br>Otherwise I've been enjoying reading about the fabulously hot Mongomerys and their extended family. 4 1/2 stars</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9945122-maria?shelf=first-in-series">first-in-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9945122-maria?shelf=maybe-another-time">maybe-another-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9945122-maria?shelf=d-n-f">d-n-f</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer538388566" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8070666411407600551"><p>I'm about 30% in on my Kindle on this, and I am debating with myself whether or not to keep going. On the one hand, I love the idea of the celebrity man/normal woman romance. It's got a certain fairytale appeal for me. I love reading those sorts of romance, which is why I wanted to read this. On the other hand... The two main characters really piss me off and I don't know if I can keep going, or whether they'll end up growing on me (like a fungus).</p><br/><br/><p>I guess what turned me off was the fact that eve</p></span>
  <span id="freeText8070666411407600551" style="display:none"><p>I'm about 30% in on my Kindle on this, and I am debating with myself whether or not to keep going. On the one hand, I love the idea of the celebrity man/normal woman romance. It's got a certain fairytale appeal for me. I love reading those sorts of romance, which is why I wanted to read this. On the other hand... The two main characters really piss me off and I don't know if I can keep going, or whether they'll end up growing on me (like a fungus).</p><br /><br /><p>I guess what turned me off was the fact that even though Natalie had no friggin clue who Luke was, or the fact that she initially thought that he was mugging her for her camera, or the fact that he is clearly keeping things from her (and she's fully aware of this fact)... She ends up at his house (alone) at the end of the day.. Um HELLO?!? I know he's a movie star... But does she??? Does she normally go to random strangers houses in the hopes of jumping their bones?? Are you really that hard up honey??</p><br /><br /><p>Luke's not any better.. His mood swings are enough to turn anyone off.. He's surprised, suspicious, joyful, horrified, sincere, wary, lustful, pissed off - Jesus Christ!! That's just the first day of meeting him... Then she goes to his house??? Just because he's hot and charming she doesn't think he's a serial killer?? I'm pretty sure Ted Bundy was described as good looking and charming too.. Didn't stop him. </p><br /><br /><p>Anyway, I might leave the story for now and probably get back to it another time... Unless someone can convince me to go on...</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="8070666411407600551" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
